## Text Elements
if I have an angle and another side with it`s
opposite angle I can find the opposite side.

If I have a side, i can find the opposite angle
with another side and it's opposite angle. ^VgS07FyT

if the function is concave up, the first derivative will be growing, if that's the case
the derivative of that will be always positive ^JOocLTRF

sequence expressed as sum of a number n times ^veRaJkgn

define the term an as an expression involving n, needs the closed form and the range ^NN921VS7

it is a type of relation that can be expressed in a sequence where each term is expressed
as some function of the previous term ^HVsQJVnK

sequence where each term is obtained by adding a constant or in closed form by adding the
constant n times plus the initial term ^aX1xT7vM

the difference obtained by subtracting the previous term to another in an arithmetic sequence.
It is therefore the constant we add with each term. ^Fof1WE4u
